<Text>Farm to Table meets a trendy Soho style backdrop...

Food and service 5/5
First off the food is locally sourced and organic...I know what you are thinking you‚Äôve heard that before...and in this case the food and the service lived up to the hype. First off the service here is super friendly and knowledgeable. My wife and I came on a Sunday morning for brunch. We came without a reservation and they quickly seated us and a server was with us. We looked over the menu and decided on the Loco Moco, chiliquies, and a side of crispy potatoes. My wife ended up ordering the Sundae Coffee and I had just a good old fashioned cup of coffee. All of the food was exceptional. The Loco moco gravy was super flavorful just the right amount of savory with the rice and the patty was tender as all can be. We finished off our brunch with a hot skillet cinnamon roll. All that I can say is that it is a like a cronut meets a cinnamon roll. It was flaky, soft, crispy, and rich all at the same time. All and all the food was very solid and right on par.

Service and decor: 5/5
As stated before the service was top notch. Our water glasses were filled up constantly and the wait staff was always coming to our table to make sure everything was going as planned. The decor is tremendous. Almost one half of the restaurant has this beautiful glass garage like door that can swing open. Giving you the feel of being outdoors but at the same time being indoors. You definitely feel like you are at a small exquisite cafe but at the same time you feel like you are in downtown SD or maybe in the Hamptons. It‚Äôs a great space!

Final thoughts...
Prep Kitchen really hits it out of the park. Upscale modern feel with homegrown farm to table food. You feel like you just stepped out of a small town and into the trendy big city. If you are in the San Marcos or North County Area definitely stop by Prep Kitchen it will be worth the trip.< /Text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN-WkpXP_j4W4SaCyXsLMJjrpckTr5V0cn1ClrV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOXQzvByimtc7QC1D-piJR2PenJ0R5YCciFiVoz=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMzO1d99TPpjCt6XQjt55PahnYUMW2-nrR-1SxP=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMorWLvM7sYvcqrhDFtWxzDaAKMtgyt8EWePkd0=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP9z4ADo7SCHDsVB3Cgz-qifSw1VLL2TEbx2tKC=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNy7EaGWZNS_wacbrPMHrGYrtiSQt229DXTj5AK=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPzW08jczEMNzQFlrm1utNSLNzFFBLq34L7mSna=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures><Response>None<//Response><Gmap_id>0x80db8bf08f877223:0x5b574dce9e1136e0<//Gmap_id></record>

Made the trip to San Marcos just try this place which had very solid food all across the board.
A) The Shrimp Tostada was packed with flavor and a spiciness that left my mouth with a delicious tingling.

<Pics>None<//Pics><UserId.>113557144647046535168<//UserId.>< review>
I rarely post reviews for products online as I'm seldom impressed with a product enough to do so.  However, in this instance I feel compelled to shout this one from the rooftops!  I am the full time caregiver for my 64 spouse who I've been married to for 46 years.  She has Type II diabetes among other serious maladies, but her blood sugar drops dangerously low without warning, often in her sleep.  With the new Libre II device monitoring her levels in real time and sounding the alarm, we are able to promptly react before she goes into hypoglycemic shock.  Just as amazing is the predictive nature of the device that forecasts rising or falling trends of her lab values thus allowing us to adjust diet and other factors resulting using less insulin.  It is a game changer for us!  Finally, we are so grateful to Advanced Diabetes Supply for guiding us through the process of obtaining the device, coordinating medical records, insurance company requirements and keeping us posted every step of the way!  We dealt with a person by the name of Izzy who was professional, compassionate and kind. Thank you from the bottom of our hearts.  Please feel free to use any or all of this review.  Terry & Carrie Herman, Preston, CT< /review>

<Text>I can't even begin to express my frustration at the incompetence of ADS. Case in point: In January 2021, I called them to update our new insurance. Diabetes supplies were not due to be refilled until March, so this gave them plenty of time.

On March 2, 2021, they sent their form text asking for authorization to ship and charge the card on file. I authorized it.

On March 12, 2021, I received an email from ADS, asking for the exact same authorization. I gave it, and asked why they were emailing when they texted for the same authorization ten days earlier.

On March 23, 2021, I called ADS to find out what was going on, because supplies were about to run out. I had to wait on hold for over TWO HOURS before I finally got to speak to someone, and they couldn't figure out what was wrong with the order.

On March 24, 2021, they called me on the phone to say that they had run the insurance verification TO THE WRONG INSURANCE. Yes, they had the correct insurance on file from when I updated it back in January, but they didn't use that one; they used the previous insurance. So now they had to run a NEW insurance verification. They assured me they'd put a rush order on it, so it should be back within a couple of days. I gave my authorization at that time for them to immediately ship it, once the verification was back.

On April 15, 2021, they called me to say that the insurance verification JUST came back (???) but wouldn't authorize a 90-day supply, which we've had for over a year. They didn't offer to send one month's supply. They didn't offer anything. Just a phone number if I wanted to call them back.

**FINAL UPDATE**
At first, I was very unhappy with ADS customer service for the reasons below. However, ADS was extremely proactive in remedying the situation and now I am extremely satisfied. As soon as my insurance approved the authorization, ADS got my order ready and out the door. I believe that my initial experience was not representative of ADS as a whole and I applaud their customer service department for going above and beyond to make sure I could get my supplies as fast as possible.

**UPDATE**
So, I'm actually really impressed with ADS customer service! Less than one day after I posted the original review, a rep contacted me and helped me get everything sorted out. It turns out we do need some more paperwork (which I found a little frustrating, because I was told multiple times by multiple reps that they had all the paperwork necessary and all I had to do was wait), but hopefully that was the last of the miscommunication. They also apologized for the lack of communication on behalf of the company and even offered to overnight me some testing materials so that I can check my blood sugars in the meantime. This interaction makes me hopeful that my previous experience with ADS was not representative of their customer service. I don't like leaving bad reviews on yelp, but I think that a company that deals with life-saving medical supplies should be held to a higher standard than say, a coffee shop. I will update this review hopefully just one more time after everything works out and I actually get my G6 system!

I've been trying to get on the Dexcom G6 and my experience with Advanced Diabetes Supply has extremely been frustrating. The process of getting the supplies I need has been delayed multiple times because different reps keep giving me the wrong information. They even sent a text message that an authorization had been submitted, but when I called to check in, it actually had not been submitted. To their credit, every rep I spoke to has been very friendly. My experience is detailed below:

ADS: "We spoke with your doctor's office yesterday, we have all the paperwork, and everything looks good. We'll give you a call when things are ready."

Me: *calls to check in two weeks later*

ADS: "Actually, we need your doctor's office to send us a form so we can send it to your insurance. After we get that, it'll take about a week for your insurance to approve it."

Me: ??? then why did you tell me everything was good and have me wait two weeks for nothing??? *Has doctor submit necessary paperwork in less than one day. calls ADS to check in a week later."

ADS: "Yes, we have all the paperwork and we just have to submit an authorization to your insurance. I'll submit it now, check back in a few days."

**They actually sent me a text message which states that the authorization was submitted as urgent and everything should be approved in about a week.

Me: *calls back a few days later to check AGAIN*

ADS: "Your authorization hasn't been submitted.... Yes, I see that someone sent you that text message, but they didn't actually submit the authorization. I'll submit it now and everything should be ready in about a week."

Me: ??????? Your company literally sent me a text message that my authorization had been submitted as "URGENT" and that I would only have to wait another week. Now my process of waiting a week is starting over??

Extremely frustrating... will be calling back tomorrow to see if they actually submitted the authorization.</Review>

This spot has had a couple different names over the last decade. Since it became Benny‚Äôs, it became perfected. A local‚Äôs favorite in the Playa Del Rey/Westchester/LMU area.

I love their rotisserie chicken. More specifically, their soup. Which comes with chunks of zucchini, carrots, cabbage and yellow squash, served with a side of Spanish rice and tortillas. For under $10. It‚Äôs so good. My husband gets their quesadillas, they are huge and a little greasy but exactly what you‚Äôre looking for in a quesadilla.

Their chips are amazing, and this is one of the few restaurants that actually gives you salsa and guacamole with their chips.

Super friendly staff who make you feel as comfortable as possible. I went to pick up an order and while waiting, they said I could chill in my car which was really nice.

If you‚Äôre a fan of Horchata or Jamaica, you‚Äôre in luck here. I usually call in orders to go.

Over 10-Car parking lot located right next to the restaurant, also plenty of street parking nearby.</text>

<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
So many great options across LA for Mexican food but Benny's is the place I consistently return to visit after visit. What's not to like? Consistently excellent rotisserie chicken to have on its own or that gets into the Mexican dishes. Fresh flavorful tacos, burritos, quesadillas, and enchiladas. Excellent sauces and side condiments. Delicious Mexican juices. Clean large outdoor patio area.  Today the choice for me were green chicken enchiladas. So delicious. I will be back again (as usual)! My friends had tacos and quesadillas. We all left happy.</Review>

< Review>
We've been here a few times and the food is pretty hit or miss, depending on the menu item. The food is either terrible or great.

The burritos are flavorless and soggy. Additionally, the nachos are an absolute disaster. The nachos do not use a queso sauce as the menu description states. The nachos are just a huge wad of cheese and meat. There are minimal chips and the whole thing was an absolutely soggy mess. We ended up throwing out most of the nachos.

Conversely, we have had the tacos and quesadillas, which were much better. Both are large and pack a lot of flavor. The real bright spot here are the chirps, which are some of the best I've ever had.< /Review>

First time here tonight and it was just alright. We started with the nacho plate to share and it was a huge disappointment. It was basically a sloppy, wet, mess. The chips were soggy and it wasn‚Äôt evenly prepared. You had a pound of guacamole that felt like thick sludge on half, tomatoes chopped on the other half with a light sprinkle of sour cream, pinto beans in between and cheese somewhere tbd. <review>One of the best local Mexican food restaurants in my area. The customer service is always excellent. The food is delicious, you can taste the quality and the care they put into cooking. They have some of the best chicken enchiladas and my mother-in-law when in town will only eat from Benny's. Any issue I've had with them, they were able to fix it and offer great customer service. It is a little bit more expensive than the other fast food Mexican restaurants, however, it is hands-down some of the best food you'll ever taste. They have fresh ingredients, it's well-balanced, well-seasoned and cooked to perfection. I've been going to Benny's for years now and ordering through Yelp and GrubHub. < Review>
I have been meaning to try Benny's! Luckily for us, we just moved to the area and I would pass by this location everyday on my way to work.

At every Mex place, I would always order huevos rancheros. Unfortunately some wouldn't have it or at least would only have it for breakfast. Not Benny's! They have it the whole day. Mine even came with chips and guacamole. My friend got a wet burrito and said it was good. It was huge that he was able to take the half home.

I appreciate the servers checking up on us in case we needed anything. Special shoutout to Jackie for hooking us up!

P.s. they have a salsa bar and dogs are welcome in their semi-outdoor seating!<//Review>

<user>101132909266086505193< /user>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>
<resp>None< /resp>< Review>
As a casual Mexican food spot, you can't get much better than Benny's in the Fox Hills/Westchester area. You order at the counter, they take your food fresh to order to eat on their patio or take to go. It can take a little while to get your food, but it's worth it to get some fresh and delicious Mexican food.

From burritos to nachos, tacos and quesadillas, Benny's has all of your favorites along with a basic salsa bar. The tortillas that they use on their burritos are really exceptional and set them apart from other Mexican joints in the area.

It's great food at a fair price. Benny's is our go-to for fast Mexican food that isn't Taco Bell in the area.</Review>

< Text>
Don't let this tiny hole in wall fool you. The tacos here are not only affordable, they are also big on flavor!

I found this taco joint via Yelp when I visited LA in January. I was looking for something close to hotel and this was only couple of blocks away. You see, I grew up in LA and there's no shortage of taco places around. What makes Benny's different from others is that they also specialize in chicken rotisserie. And that's one of the tacos I ordered together with the Carnitas and Al Pastor.

Now, let's talk about quality. The Carnitas was super moist and tasty and the achiote marinated pork from the Al Pastor was full of flavor. Surprisingly, the Rotisserie Chicken taco was also juicy and delicious. I know its just chicken but this was done right. Prices were reasonable too. Tacos started at $3.50 each and goes up to $4.25 for the shrimp.

For around $12, I had a satisfying lunch at Benny's. It's casual, people are nice and not stingy with the meat.<//Text>

< review>
Im a taco connoisseur. So when this place was recommended, i drove the extra miles to experience the hype.
The location is great but could use more parking...Especially with the option to sit and eat. I love the outdoor patio area.
The Aqua fresca drinks are delicious. The condiments bar is a huge plus. Customer service was great and service was pretty fast.
Unfortunately, i was not as pleased with the tacos. I ordered 3 shrimp, 3 Carne Asada and 2 watermelon drinks. My charge was almost $30. With that alone, i just knew my experience was going to be amazing. It was nothing to write home about. The chipotle sauce for the shrimp tacos actually makes the taco. I will stick to my local street vendors.</review>
